### Astro-TE NN_1 Jph4 astrocyte (Mmus) `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307041`
#### Removed
- [Astro-TE NN_1 Jph4 astrocyte (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307041) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Myoc (Mmus), Sptbn2 (Mmus), Alpk1 (Mmus) expressing astrocyte of brain (Mus musculus)"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Astro-TE NN_1 Jph4 astrocyte (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307041) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A astrocyte of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Myoc (Mmus), Sptbn2 (Mmus), Alpk1 (Mmus). It is distinguished from other Astro-TE NN_1 cells by expression of Myoc, Jph4, Alpk1. It is glutamatergic. These cells are located in the Isocortex, brain . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. (2023), Whole Mouse Brain in cell set Cluster:5221 Astro-TE NN_1."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "https://doi.org/10.1038/s41586-023-06812-z"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

#### Added
- [Astro-TE NN_1 Jph4 astrocyte (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307041) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A astrocyte of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Myoc (Mmus), Sptbn2 (Mmus), Alpk1 (Mmus). It is distinguished from other Astro-TE NN_1 cells by expression of Myoc, Jph4, Alpk1. It is glutamatergic (inferred from expression of Aldh1a1, Slc17a7). These cells are located in the Isocortex, brain . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. (2023), Whole Mouse Brain in cell set Cluster:5221 Astro-TE NN_1."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "https://doi.org/10.1038/s41586-023-06812-z"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Astro-TE NN_1 Jph4 astrocyte (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307041) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Location is inferred from registration of MerFish Data. Registration may be inaccurate, giving misleading location to adjacent anatomical regions."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### CB PLI GABA Ly6d Purkinje layer interneuron `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307005`
#### Removed
- [CB PLI GABA Ly6d Purkinje layer interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307005) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Ly6d (Mmus), Kit (Mmus) expressing Purkinje layer interneuron of brain (Mus musculus)"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [CB PLI GABA Ly6d Purkinje layer interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307005) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A Purkinje layer interneuron of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Ly6d (Mmus), Kit (Mmus). It is distinguished from other CB PLI Gly-Gaba cells by expression of Ly6d. It is GABAergic. These cells are located in the Cerebellum, brain , in or close to the regions: arbor vitae, Interposed nucleus, Nodulus (X) . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. (2023), Whole Mouse Brain in cell set Cluster:5185 CB PLI Gly-Gaba_4."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "https://doi.org/10.1038/s41586-023-06812-z"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [CB PLI GABA Ly6d Purkinje layer interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307005) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Warning: Despite its name, CB PLI Gly-Gaba_4 does not secrete the neurotransmitter Gly, as assessed by expression of multiple marker genes."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

#### Added
- [CB PLI GABA Ly6d Purkinje layer interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307005) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A Purkinje layer interneuron of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Ly6d (Mmus), Kit (Mmus). It is distinguished from other CB PLI Gly-Gaba cells by expression of Ly6d. It is GABAergic (inferred from expression of Gad1, Gad2, Slc32a1). These cells are located in the Cerebellum, brain , in or close to the regions: arbor vitae, Interposed nucleus, Nodulus (X) . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. (2023), Whole Mouse Brain in cell set Cluster:5185 CB PLI Gly-Gaba_4."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "https://doi.org/10.1038/s41586-023-06812-z"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### DCO Il22 Gly-Gaba_2 cerebellar neuron (Mmus) `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4306992`
#### Removed
- [DCO Il22 Gly-Gaba_2 cerebellar neuron (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4306992) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Il22 (Mmus), Edaradd (Mmus) expressing cerebellar neuron of brain (Mus musculus)"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [DCO Il22 Gly-Gaba_2 cerebellar neuron (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4306992) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A cerebellar neuron of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Il22 (Mmus), Edaradd (Mmus). It is distinguished from other DCO Il22 Gly-Gaba cells by expression of Ppp1r17. It is GABAergic and glycinergic. These cells are located in the Medulla, Cerebellum, brain , in or close to the regions: Paraflocculus, arbor vitae, Dorsal cochlear nucleus . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. (2023), Whole Mouse Brain in cell set Cluster:5172 DCO Il22 Gly-Gaba_2."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "https://doi.org/10.1038/s41586-023-06812-z"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

#### Added
- [DCO Il22 Gly-Gaba_2 cerebellar neuron (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4306992) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A cerebellar neuron of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Il22 (Mmus), Edaradd (Mmus). It is distinguished from other DCO Il22 Gly-Gaba cells by expression of Ppp1r17. It is GABAergic and glycinergic (inferred from expression of Slc32a1, Hdc, Slc6a5, Gad2, Gad1). These cells are located in the Medulla, Cerebellum, brain , in or close to the regions: Paraflocculus, arbor vitae, Dorsal cochlear nucleus . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. (2023), Whole Mouse Brain in cell set Cluster:5172 DCO Il22 Gly-Gaba_2."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

- [Island of Calleja granule cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4030053) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A GABAergic neuron that resides in the islands of calleja and shows the cytoarchitectural and molecular features characteristic of this granule-like cell population. In mice and primates, it expresses D1 and D3 dopamine receptors (Drd1; Drd3), GABAergic markers (GAD1/2) and form densely packed granule cell clusters in the olfactory tubercle within the ventral striatum. Moreover it receives dense dopaminergic input from the VTA, and functionally associated with self-grooming behaviors and depression-like behaviors."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34795450"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "doi:10.1016/j.cub.2021.10.015"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### Tanycyte NN_2 Mylk3 alpha1-tanycyte (Mmus) `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307065`
#### Removed
- [Tanycyte NN_2 Mylk3 alpha1-tanycyte (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307065) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Dynlrb2 (Mmus), Mylk3 (Mmus), Sfta3-ps (Mmus) expressing alpha1-tanycyte of brain (Mus musculus)"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Tanycyte NN_2 Mylk3 alpha1-tanycyte (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4307065) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A alpha1-tanycyte of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Dynlrb2 (Mmus), Mylk3 (Mmus), Sfta3-ps (Mmus). It is distinguished from other Tanycyte NN_2 cells by expression of Mylk3. It is glutamatergic. These cells are located in the Hypothalamus , in or close to the regions: Periventricular hypothalamic nucleus, intermediate part . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. ### dermal sheath fibroblast `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020013`

#### Added
- Class: [dermal sheath fibroblast](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020013) 

- [dermal sheath fibroblast](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020013) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0009-0000-8480-9277](https://orcid.org/0009-0000-8480-9277) 

- [dermal sheath fibroblast](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020013) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0020013"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [dermal sheath fibroblast](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020013) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A fibroblast forming the connective tissue sheath that encloses the hair follicle epithelium from the level of the bulge downward to the hair bulb. This cell expresses characteristic markers, including DPEP1 in humans and COL11A1 and ACTA2 (alpha-smooth muscle actin) in mice and humans. Dermal sheath fibroblast possesses contractile properties mediated by calcium-calmodulin-myosin light chain kinase signalling, generating centripetal force during hair follicle catagen that relocates the dermal papilla to the stem cell niche."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:35069694"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31857493"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [dermal sheath fibroblast](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020013) [has_related_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym) "DS fibroblast"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

- [fibroblast of the reticular layer of dermis](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_2000096) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A fibroblast of dermis that resides in the deep reticular layer, characterised by robust extracellular matrix production with high type I collagen deposition forming densely packed, organised fibrillar networks (Ghetti et al., 2018). - [hair follicle dermal stem cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072103) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A bipotent mesenchymal stem cell that resides in the dermal sheath, specifically within the dermal sheath cup at the base of the hair follicle, characterized by its capacity for self-renewal and differentiation into both dermal sheath and dermal papilla cells throughout hair cycling. In humans, this cell is marked by enriched expression of gremlin-2 (GREM2) and dipeptidase-1 (DPEP1), and acts as a progenitor reservoir sustaining and regenerating the follicle's mesenchymal compartments."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### hypothalamic gonadotropin-releasing hormone neuron (Mmus) `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4304384`

- [hypothalamic gonadotropin-releasing hormone neuron (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4304384) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Gnrh1 (Mmus) expressing hypothalamic gonadotropin-releasing hormone neuron of brain (Mus musculus)"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [hypothalamic gonadotropin-releasing hormone neuron (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4304384) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A hypothalamic gonadotropin-releasing hormone neuron of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Gnrh1 (Mmus). It is glutamatergic. These cells are located in the Hypothalamus, Olfactory areas, Pallidum, brain , in or close to the regions: Lateral septal nucleus, rostral (rostroventral) part, Medial septal nucleus, Diagonal band nucleus . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. (2023), Whole Mouse Brain in cell set Cluster:2564 HY Gnrh1 Glut_1."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

#### Added
- [hypothalamic gonadotropin-releasing hormone neuron (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4304384) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A hypothalamic gonadotropin-releasing hormone neuron of the Mus musculus brain. It is distinguished from other cells in the brain by selective expression of Gnrh1 (Mmus). It is glutamatergic (inferred from expression of Gad1, Slc17a6, Gad2). These cells are located in the Hypothalamus, Olfactory areas, Pallidum, brain , in or close to the regions: Lateral septal nucleus, rostral (rostroventral) part, Medial septal nucleus, Diagonal band nucleus . Reference transcriptomic data for this type can be found in the dataset/taxonomy - Yao et al. (2023), Whole Mouse Brain in cell set Cluster:2564 HY Gnrh1 Glut_1."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### intrinsically photosensitive retinal ganglion cell `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020014`

#### Added
- Class: [intrinsically photosensitive retinal ganglion cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020014) 

- [intrinsically photosensitive retinal ganglion cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020014) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/creator) "GitHub Copilot"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [intrinsically photosensitive retinal ganglion cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020014) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0000-0003-2473-2313](https://orcid.org/0000-0003-2473-2313) 

- [intrinsically photosensitive retinal ganglion cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020014) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0009-0000-8480-9277](https://orcid.org/0009-0000-8480-9277) 

- [intrinsically photosensitive retinal ganglion cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020014) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0020014"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [intrinsically photosensitive retinal ganglion cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020014) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A retinal ganglion cell that is intrinsically photosensitive, functioning as a non-image-forming photoreceptor, distinguished from rod and cone photoreceptors by the expression of the photopigment melanopsin in mice and humans (Hattar et al., 2002; Tri Hoang Do &amp; Yau, 2015). Located primarily in the ganglion cell layer with some displaced somata in the inner nuclear layer, this neuron depolarises directly in response to environmental irradiance (Tri Hoang Do &amp; Yau, 2015). It projects via the retinohypothalamic tract to central targets, including the suprachiasmatic nucleus (SCN) for circadian photoentrainment and the olivary pretectal nucleus (OPN) for the pupillary light reflex."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "Wikipedia:Intrinsically_photosensitive_retinal_ganglion_cell"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)
